<userid>107325830037888892486</userid><Name>Teddy S.< /Name><date>1603602485748<//date><rating>5<//rating>< Text>
This is a no-frills a grocery store with great produce, including a wide selection of figs including plantains,bananas, and burros and they always have a wide selection of lemons and limes at great prices. They also have a prepared food section nestled next to the butcher where you can pick up tonight's dinner. Chicharrones are also available which I have yet to try but there's always great interest. There's not much in selection as far as pantry items go. The brands lean more towards those found in the southern part of the continent. I mostly come here for the produce and for the great salsa music that they have playing in the background. It adds a nice touch. The cashiers have barriers. Ask for the Corona...They wear gloves and everyone's social distanced; markers are on the floor and everyone is required to wear masks. All the baskets and carts actually I don't think they have carts but all the baskets are sanitized. They also take Google pay. It's in a strip mall so there's plenty of parking!</Text>

<Review>My wife and I try to get to Laguna Beach ever year to enjoy the vibe, food and surf. While here we tend to stay close to our hotel or eat at Nicks where its hard to beat their petit filet mingon. But today, to celebrate the lifting of the dark cloud that has enveloped America for the last four years, we decided to check out A & O Kitchen and Bar restaurant at the Balboa Bay Resort that was near to where we took a stroll. Though not inexpensive, the food and service, were well worth the cost. Victoria H., our waitress, was fantastic as well. We started with some champagne, as I said we were celebrating, and then enjoyed a bottle of red wine. I fully enjoyed my perfectly seasoned steak served at the perfect temperature while my wife couldnt stop telling me how great her lobster roll was. For dessert she had the carrot cake while I splurged, calorie wise, on the pot de creme with a shot of Grand Marnier. Well worth the calories. The unobstructed views weren't bad either. Though youll have to ask to be seated in the one of two lilliputian greenhouses along side the boat dock. Truly a unique experience.< /Review><Pictures>None</Pictures><Response>None< /Response>< gmapID>

<review>Came here to check out their Newport Beach Restaurant week menu. Food was ok. Service was on the slower side on a Holiday- MLK day.

For $20 the value of the 2-course lunch was good.

I had the tuna poke for appetizer and it was a miss. The tuna didnt taste super fresh. It was on top of some guac. The whole thing was on the mushy side. It was served with fried wontons that were crispy but felt oily.

For entree I had the Fish tacos. They came in 2, with a good sized piece of fish, and topped with cabbage. Not bad but nothing that I would go out of my way to have again.

If you sit outside, you can see the water and  the boats. Inside was fine and there were birds flying around which was a bit distracting.

They validate your valet parking.

I was hoping we could do some walking with a view but there isnt much to walk around.

Overall, experience was fine but would probably not return.< /review>< pics>

After searching my pockets without asking or explaining y they start to search the car again without asking or explaining themselves. I asked the copportunity if she thought I was stupid. Why would I steal something right in front of am employee and then sit in my car for 10 or 15 min waiting on the cops to show up. <Review>We used to frequent this restaurant quite a bit but we noticed the menu was changed and the quality of the food wasn't the same. The steak sandwiches were tough and grissley. My husband's favorite chicken sandwich was eliminated all together. On Monday, 04November we went to the Elephant Bar in San Marcos for dinner. There were very few diners there and I thought it would be busier because of Monday night football. I was with my husband and a close friend. My friend and I ordered the steak sandwich and my friend ordered a salad with no croutons. I ordered a med rare steak. My husband ordered a chicken sandwich with no bbq sauce. First of all, the food came out extremely late for an empty restaurant. The waitress was a beautiful petite, dark brunette who was a professional at her job and extremely nice. My friend's salad came out with croutons on it, no big deal there. My steak came out Medium to done so I sent it back. The steak came back again extremely bloody rare. I sent it back again and the third time was perfect. My husband's chicken sandwich had bbq sauce on it and the waitress realized it and said they were making another sandwich for him. But when it came, they scraped off the bbq sauce off the meat and my husband could still taste the sauce. He wasn't happy with the order at all. It was obvious that the cooks weren't paying much attention to the order the waitress was giving them. Or they had new cooks. How can you mess up on a medium rare steak that many times? <text>Incredible Park that has seen dramatic improvements over the past few years. To name a few: brand new Olympic sized swimming pool that is kept in excellent condition, 2 brand new full sized basketball courts with smooth paving, updated playground for children.

Other amenities include 2 full tennis courts, soccer fields, baseball diamonds, and a skate park. In my opinion no other neighborhood park in LA County comes close.  There is plenty of room for everyone and the grounds are kept up.

My only recommendation would be to install some water fountains that also include a dog fountain at the bottom since so many people walk their dogs there.

There is also the South side of the park that is below the 60 freeway that can be accessed via foot bridge. It includes a large pond that is stocked with fish to enjoy fishing and a small ampitheatre.

To the gentleman who posted a review regarding no shade on the playground, I disagree, the playground and park itself is surrounded with plenty of trees.<//text>< response>

The place is managed by an "idiocracy", which is of course, idiots running a bureaucracy. If you go there in the middle of the day to swim, it's free, but you cannot go in the deep end unless you take a swim test every single time. And you CANNOT wear flip flops walking out to the pool. BUT, if you wait a few hours and pay them $2 to swim in the evening, you MUST wear flip-flops and you can ONLY swim in the deep end, but no swim test required. The pool is really nice, but I won't be back. Their rules are just too idiotic and confusing.< /Text>
